remarks:
remarks:        You may use BGP Standard or Large Communities to
remarks:        control route redistribution via the route servers:
remarks:
remarks:        (56890:56890), (56890:1:0): Redistribute to all route server peers (default)
remarks:        (56890:<peer ASN>), (56890:1:56890): Redistribute to <peer ASN>
remarks:        (0:<peer ASN>), (56890:0:<peer ASN>): Do not redistribute to <peer ASN>
remarks:        (0:56890), (56890:0:0): Do not redistribute
remarks:
remarks:        If <peer ASN> uses a 16b ASN, you may use BGP Standard or Large Communities
remarks:        If <peer ASN> uses a 32b ASN, you have to use BGP Large Communities
remarks:
remarks:        There are additional communities for controlling announcements:
remarks:
remarks:        65535:0 GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN
remarks:        65535:666 BLACKHOLE
remarks:        56890:65281 NO-EXPORT
remarks:        56890:65282 NO-ADVERTISE
remarks:
remarks:        For more information on route server control and blackholing, please see:
remarks:        https://docs.de-cix.net/category/jyc0p3ubp9
